 kisi jamaane main ek bombai hua karti thi
 Fairytale city yah jameen kaa vah falak tha jahaan myth or yatharth kaa, kuwwat or kalpana kaa, ummid or tafarih kaa sangam hua tha
 This was our top city
 yah desh kaa aarthik hriday or sabhyataa kii jaan tha
 For the rest of the country, it was a world of imagination covered with bright pages, where anything was possible
 yahaan ke bashindon ke liye yah dhandhe se hankey jate sapanom kaa shikhar tha, jahaan bas peeth ghumaate hi agali chalaang takadir badal detii
 Delhi was a refugee colony, whose fabric was woven from Karstani after the fall of the Mughals
 desh kii pehali sudur shahari basti kolkata hukumat ke lihaaj se namufeed jagah par hone or naksalwad ke ubhaar se tahas-nahas ho gai

 yahaan ke sthaneey logon ke liye bombai yaa mumbai hameshaa baahar se aakar basane waalon kaa shahar tha

 lekin ve hindustan kii duusari jagahon par baahar se jaakar basane waalon se alahada the

 log bas stand par or elistaron ke baahar tahjeeb se khadey rahete

 unki hedlite hameshaa lo beam par hotin

 khara, magar donon baanhen failaakar swaagat karne vaala

 yani dere dalit matadaataaon kaa acha khaasaa vot bank he
